a wannan makon kaɗai babban layin lantarki na ƙasa ya lalace har sau biyu bayan yab lalace sau uku cikin kwana biyu a watan oktoba

babban layin ya lalace sau 10 jimilla a shekarar 2024 abin da ke jefa kusan dukkan ƙasar cikin duhu duk lokacin da hakan ta faru

kazalika har yanzu yan arewacin ƙasar ba su gama farfaɗowa daga asarar da suka tafka ba sakamakon katsewar wutar a yankin aƙalla tsawon kwana 10 na ƙarshen watan oktoba

masu sharhi na cewa sabuwar dokar lantarki ta 2023 da aka sanya wa hannu ta faɗaɗa damar samarwa da kuma rarraba wutar musamman ga gwamnatocin jiha saɓanin a baya da gwamnatin tarayya ce kaɗai ke da alhakin yin hakan

bayanai sun nuna cewa najeriya na iya samar da wuta 3000mw zuwa 5000mw a kullum daga cikin 13000mw da za ta iya samarwa daga

kusan kashi 75 cikin 100 na samuwa ne daga iskar gas sai kuma mafi yawa na sauran 35 ɗin daga madatsun ruwa

rahotonni sun nuna cewa tuni wasu gwamnatocin jiha suka fara yunƙurin samar wa kan su wutar

asalin hotonreuters a najeriya jihar legas ce kan gaba wajen samar da lantarki a cikin gida kuma hakan ba abi mamaki ba ne saboda ita ce mafi girman tattalin arziki tsakanin jihohin ƙasar 36

ita ce jihar da ke da ke da maaikata musamman ta makamashi ministry of energy mineral resources da kuma hukumar kula da lantarki lagos state electricity board

tsakanin shekarun 2011 zuwa 2015 lseb ta dasa tashoshin samar da wuta huɗu da zimmar inganta wutar a gidaje da kuma samar da haske a tituna

ɗaya daga cikin tanadetanaden sabuwar lantarkin shi ne bai wa ɗaiɗaikun mutane da kamfanoni damar samar da lantarki

a watan agustan 2024 ne hukumar kula da lantarki ta najeriya nigerian electricity regulatory commission nerc ta bai wa kamfanin sadarwa na mtn lasisin samar da lantarkin mai ƙarfin 15 94mw a jihar ta legas

nerc ta ce lasisin da ta bai wa kamfanin da wasu huɗu na amfanin kansu ne ba don sayar wa kwastomomi ba kuma za su samar da wutar ne a jihohin legas da oyo da ogun da cross river

za su samar da jimillar lantarki mai ƙarfin109 69mw

a watan mayun 2024 ita ma gwamnatin jihar kano ƙarƙashin gwamna abba kabir yusuf ta sanar da kafa wani kwamati da zai yi nazari tare da ƙirƙiro dokar da za ta kula da ɓangaren lantarki a jihar

yayin wata ziyara a ofishin hukumar kula da lantarki ta ƙasa ranar 9 ga watan mayun tawagar ta bayyana cewa tana fatan dokar da suke sa ran ƙirƙirowa za ta taimaka wajen inganta wutar da ɗumbin alummar jihar ke samu musamman ga masanaantu

a ranar alhamis da ta gabata ne kuma gwamnan jihar ekiti da ke kudancin najeriya biodun oyebanji ya bayar da sanarwar cewa gwamnatinsa ta bai wa wasu kamfanoni lasisin samarwa da rarraba lantarki a jihar

wata sanarwa da gwamnan ya wallafa a shafinsa na sada zumunta ta ce rukunin kamfanoni huɗu suka bai wa lasisin zuwa yanzu

wannan yunƙuri zai inganta hanyoyin samarwa da rarraba wuta da kuma samar da mitocin wuta ga mazauna jihar a cewar sanarwar

ya tabbatar da cewa jiharsa ta ekiti na samun mega watt 20 zuwa 25 daga babban layin lantarki na ƙasa wanda ya gaza daga 120 mw da suke buƙata

a cewarsa burinmu shi ne mu kai 130 mw ta hanyar gina ƙaƙƙarfan layi da zai sa mu rage dogaro da layi na ƙasa kamar yadda dokar lantarki ta 2023 ta tanada

abin da ya kamata su gane shi ne allah ya albarkace ɓangaren da muka fito arewacin najeriya da ƙarfin zafin rana ana cewa za a iya samun wuta ta tsawon awa tara daga ƙarfin ranar da ake da shi a yankin in ji ta

ta ƙara da cewa tun da daɗewa wasu jihohi a kudancin najeriya suka fara samar da yanayin da za su inganta lantarki a jihohin ta hanyar haɗaka da yankasuwa

both variants of metatrader have unique features and tools that endear them to the african trading public though a few challenges have been pinpointed trading platforms serve as a traders workplace and the coming of metatrader 4 and 5 into the african financial landscape has been a huge blessing in the black continent

both variants of metatrader have unique features and tools that endear them to the african trading public though a few challenges have been pinpointed

metatrader is described as an online thirdparty trading platform foreign exchange traders leverage in trading forex futures and contracts for differences cfds

metaquotes software corp a russian software company is the developer of metatrader which comes in two variants

the first variant of the trading platform is metatrader 4 or mt4

themetatrader 4 appwas developed in 2005 and the second variant metatrader 5 or mt5 was launched in 2010 with more robust features and tools

below are some of the numerous opportunities african traders stand to reap from using the meta trader 4 and meta trader 5 platforms

since they were released in 2005 and 2010 respectively both mt4 metatrader 4 and mt5 metatrader 5 have debuted in the competitive african financial market and are making their present felt by multiasset traders trading instruments like commodities cfds stocks futures bonds and options

as they are gradually getting integrated into the african financial landscape these two industrystandard platforms present multiasset traders in the continent with a lot of opportunities to explore

while mt4 is generally associated with forex trading this variant of metatrader has proved to be equally robust for trading in several other markets such ascryptocurrenciesindices commodities and more

it achieves this through cfd contract for difference trading

this multifeature nature of mt4 has benefited multiple investors in the african financial market who explore these markets

traders in the african financial landscape are enjoying the free services of mt4 all they need do is to download the platform and install it without paying any upfront cost

however they would have to go through financial brokers who may have a few minor charges and may also incur some tradingassociated costs including commissions spreads and brokers charges

the broker charges tend to vary depending on things like the trading account a trader chooses and the broker

important to note that there are brokers who offer premium or improved versions of the metatrader 4 platform to traders

while the premium version comes complete with additional tools and advanced features it may attract additional fees

mt4 is a highly customizable platform that offers african investors opportunities to tailor its tools and features to their individual needs

the platform leverages predefined parameters to support algorithmic trading

african traders who choose to do their business on metatrader have above 30 builtin technical indicators at their disposal which makes for flexibility in trading

with the aid of indicators like macd rsi and fibonacci retracements traders in the african markets are better equipped to analyze the movement of prices across different timeframes

the markets offered by metatrader 5 are more extended than what is obtainable in mt4

themetatrader 5 appgoes way beyond forex and allows traders access to financial instruments like stocks commodities and futures

through the big communities offered by both platforms traders connect to each other find additional tools and resources and help themselves get better

the mt5 community is called the mql5 community and it comes a bit livelier than mt4 offering its traders additional support through webinars and tutorials

it also features a special unit on the metaquotes website specifically for mql programming

in addition the advanced feature of mt5 offers traders enhanced charting additional order types and more timeframes suitable for automated and manual trading

both mt4 and mt5 have come to stay in the african financial landscape and have managed to establish a strong devoted client base in the black continent despite the teething challenges they faced in their early days

with its userfriendly interface and focus on binary options trading quotex offers opportunities for profit as thepopularity of online tradingcontinues to rise platforms like quotex have captured the attention of both new and seasoned traders alike

with its userfriendly interface and focus on binary options trading quotex offers opportunities for profit but also comes with its own set of challenges

before you dive into trading on quotex its crucial to arm yourself with the right knowledge and understanding

heres what you need to know before you begin

at its core quotex specializes in binary options trading a form of trading that allows you to predict the price movement of various assets such as currencies commodities and stocks over a specified time frame

the mechanics are simple you choose whether you believe the price will rise a call option or fall a put option within that timeframe

if your prediction is correct you earn a fixed return if not you lose your investment in that trade

despite its straightforward nature binary options trading requires careful analysis and strategic planning

before you start trading on quotex developing a comprehensive trading plan is essential

your trading plan should outline your goals risk tolerance and specific strategies you intend to use

consider the following when crafting your plan 1

goals explain what you want to accomplish by trading

are you looking for shortterm gains or longterm investment growth

having clear goals will help you make better choices 2

risk management determine how much capital youre willing to risk on each trade

a common recommendation is to risk only 12 of your total trading capital per trade

this approach helps to protect your account from significant losses 3

asset selection identify which assets you want to trade

different assets come with varying levels of volatility and market behavior so understanding the characteristics of each will inform your trading strategy

one of the most valuable features of quotex is its demo account

this option allows you to practice trading with virtual funds providing a riskfree environment to familiarize yourself with the platform

use the demo account to experiment with different trading strategies understand how various indicators work and build your confidence without the pressure of real financial stakes

its an invaluable tool for both beginners and experienced traders looking to refine their skills

successful trading on quotex relies heavily on effective market analysis

understanding both technical and fundamental analysis is key to making informed trading decisions

technical analysis this involves studying price charts and using indicators to identify trends and patterns

familiarize yourself with common indicators such as moving averages rsi relative strength index and bollinger bands

these tools can help you determine optimal entry and exit points for your trades

fundamental analysis this focuses on economic news and events that can impact asset prices

stay informed about economic indicators interest rates and geopolitical events that could affect the markets

being aware of these factors can provide valuable insights into potential price movements

trading can evoke a wide range of emotions from excitement during winning trades to frustration during losses

keeping control of your emotions is very important for achieve lasting success

here are some tips to manage your emotions while trading 1

stick to your plan resist the temptation to deviate from your trading plan based on emotions

if a trade doesnt go as expected analyze it calmly rather than reacting impulsively 2

avoid chasing losses its easy to fall into the trap of trying to recover losses quickly

this can lead to poor decisionmaking

take the time to evaluate your strategies and learn from your mistakes instead 3

take breaks if you find yourself feeling overwhelmed or frustrated take a step back

taking breaks can help clear your mind and prevent emotional trading

the financial markets are constantly changing and staying informed is crucial for success

take advantage of the educational resources available on quotex such as tutorials webinars and market analysis

engaging with trading communities can also provide insights and strategies from other traders

continuous learning allows you to adapt to changing market conditions and refine your trading approach

trading on quotex offers a unique opportunity toengage in binary options trading but its essential to approach it with a wellinformed mindset

by understanding the fundamentals of binary options developing a solid trading plan utilizing the demo account and conducting thorough market analysis you can enhance your chances of success

remember to maintain emotional discipline and commit to continuous learning

with the right preparation and strategy quotex can become a valuable platform on your trading journey

happy trading

hasken dare a lagos bai taka kara ya karya ba idan aka kwatanta da johannesburg singapore dubai ko london

amma abinda nake son nunawa shi ne hasken dare kamar kanun labarai adadin kuɗaɗen da ake tarawa a cikin gida adadi da salon kaɗa ƙuria yawan yaran da suke zuwa makaranta ƙaruwar yawan alumma da sauransu zai iya haska mana alƙibla da ci gaban jihohi biyun da suka fi yawan jamaa a najeriya

kanun labarai daga jihohin biyu a makon jiya sun isa misali

a lagos babban labarin shi ne shugaba bola ahmed tinubu ya ƙaddamar da layin jirgin ƙasa na cikin gari mai suna red line wanda a cewar gwamna babajide sanwoolu zai yi jigilar fasinja 500000 a kullum

a kano labari ake na hisba wata hukumar kula da tarbiyya da ta kasa samun gurbin zama a hukumance ko a aikace ko kuma samun tasiri a cikin alumma

akwai kamanceceniya sosai a tsakaninsu

duk suna da muhimmin tasiri a siyasar najeriya

su ne jihohin da suka fi yawan alumma da kuma ƙabilu dabamdabam

a nan zaka ga jikokin an yemen syria lebanon afirka ta arewa chad mali nijar da ƙabilun kanuri yoruba nupe edo da ma wasu da dama balle a zo batun fulani da sauran hausawa da suka zama halattattun kanawa masu harshe ɗaya aƙida ɗaya sanadiyyar tsawon zama da auratayya tsakaninsu

a 1999 lagos ta ɗauki kanta a matsayin cibiyar tattalin arzikin najeriya kuma shugabanninta suka ɗau hanyar da za su ƙara ƙaimi a wannan ɓangare

tun a 1999 suka fara maganar samar da wutar lantarki ta su ta kansu samar da manyan motocin sufuri jirgin ƙasa na cikin gari wadatar da alumma da gidaje tashar jiragen sama a tsibirin lagos babbar gada ta huɗu da kuma mayar da unguwannin matalauta dake tsakiyar birnin zuwa halattattun cibiyoyin kasuwanci

kawo yanzu basu cimma waɗannan manufofin ba amma tinƙistinƙis suna kan hanya yayinda gwamnoni ke ɗorawa daga inda magabatansu suka tsaya tare da bunƙasa tattalin arzikin jihar aƙalla idan aka kwatanta da sauran jiohin najeriya koda a wasu lokutan hakan na sa jihar ta yi tahomugama da gwamnatin tarayya

amma dai tsarin ya biya buƙata kuma sakamakon ya bayyana a zahiri koda kuwa da sauransu idan aka kwatanta da sauran sassan duniya

amma labarin ya sha bamban a kano

a 1999 babu wanda yake kokwanton kano ce cibiyar tattalin arzikin arewacin najeriya kuma ta biyu ga lagos a faɗin ƙasar nan

sai dai a farkon shekarun 2000 sai alƙiblar ta fara sauyawa

a yanzu ita ce ta takwas a samun kuɗin shiga cikin jihohin najeriya yayinda lagos ta riƙe kambunta har ma ta ƙara tazarar dake tsakaninta da sauran jihohi

don kuwa maimkon kano ta gina kanta a matsayin cibiyar kasuwanci ta arewa kuma ta biyu a najeriya sai ta nemi ta zama jihar da tafi musulunci a tsakanin jihohin musulmin arewacin najeriya ko me hakan ke nufi a najeriyar da dama fiye da rabinta musulmi ne

maimakon a kalli sufuri a matsayin wata hanyar inganta harkokin kasuwanci sai aka ɗauke shi a matsayin wani nauyi na addini domin samun damar hana maza da mata cakuɗa a cikin abin hawa ta hanyar samar da babur mai ƙafa uku da aka raɗawa sunan da ya dace da shi na adaidaita sahu

wato maimakon a yi tunanin sababbin hanyoyin da za a shigar da mata cikin harkokin kasuwanci kamar yadda turkey indonesia da sauran ƙasashen musulmi suka yi sai aka ga zai fi kyau a ƙara killace su daga idon jamaa da kuma harkokin kasuwancin

kuma maimakon aci albarkacin damar da harshen hausa ya bayar na zama harshen yammacin afirka a fitar da abubuwan gargajiya zuwa kasuwannin duniya sai aka ɓuge da kafa hisbah da hukumar tace finafinai

bugu da ƙari yayin da siyasar lagos ke da manufa a jiha da tarayya kano ta na gudanar da siyasa da take cikin waɗanda suka fi rashin samar da riba a najeriya

a duk zaɓuɓɓukan shugaban ƙasa tun daga 1999 mutanen kano suna tuttuɗo ƙuriun da suka nunka na lagos sai dai jagororin jihar ba su gano yadda za su yi amfani da wannan damar su kawo mata cigaba ba sai dai samarwa waɗansu an tsirari muƙaman siyasa

siyasar cikin gida ma tafi haka lalacewa

daga washegarin ranar zaɓe har zuwa jajiberin zaɓe mai zuwa bayan shekaru huɗu kullum mutane na shiga gidajen rediyo suna fafatawa a fagen siyasa a madadin wani ubangidansu akan wani abu maras amfani

babu wani waje a faɗin najeriya da ake tattauna siyasa akaiakai kamar kano amma ba sa haifar da komai sai dai gadar sama a nan gadar ƙasa a can abinda ya zama tsarin samar da kayan more rayuwa da sauran jihohi arewa suke kwaikwaya

mutane uku ne suka mulki kano daga mayu 1999 zuwa mayu 2023

amma zazzafar adawar dake tsakaninsu da tsakanin magoya bayansu da kuma yadda kullum ake bayyanar da wannan adawar sun jawo babu abinda ake samu a kano face siyasar rashin cigaba ko kuma ace siyasar surutu don dai ace an ce

sai dai har yanzu kano na fuskantar ƙalubalen haɓaka zuwa tsarin tattalin arziki na zamani wutar lantarki ta kan ta haɓaka sufuri wadatar da alumma da gidaje ƙarin ƙwararrun mutane da ayyukan ƙwararru da kuma dawo da masanaantu ta yadda za su yi kankankan da rukunonin shaguna

haka kuma akwai ƙalubalen dawo da martabarta a matsayin cibiyar bunƙasar tattalin arziki ta arewa da kuma siyasa mai manufa da shugabanci nagari don samun wannan sauyin da ake buƙata

a mataki na farko ya zama wajibi ga shugabannin kano su kawo wani sabon tsarin siyasa mai sauƙin kacenace da kuma manufar haɓaka tattalin arziki ta tsawon aƙalla kimanin shekaru 25 wadda duk gwamnatin da aka zaɓa ita za ta bi kuma a kanta za ta jagoranci mutane ba tare da laakari da bambancin jamiyya ba

abu na biyu ya zama wajibi kano ta samo hanyar da zata ci gajiyar ɗimbin ƙuriun da take kaɗawa a siyasar ƙasa wurin janyo tallafin gwamnatin tarayya domin ci gaban jihar da kuma ɗabbaƙa manufar jihar ta bunƙasa masanaantu alal misali

na uku kuma mafi muhimmanci wajibi ne jihar kano ta ɗora ɗimbin kasuwancin da ake yi a cikinta bisa tsari na zamani domin samun ƙarin haraji da kuɗin shiga ga gwamnatin

duk waɗannan abubuwa ne masu yiwuwa amma akwai buƙatar abubuwan da suka zarta hukumar hisba da baburan adaidaita sahu

mijin ya daɓa wa matar wuƙa kuma ya kulle ta a ɗaki sannan ya banka mata wuta inda ya raunata kansa

wani magidanci mai shekara 30 mai suna motunrayo olaniyi ya daɓa wa sabuwar amaryarsa mai suna olajumoke wuƙa lamarin da ya yi sanadiyar mutuwarta

lamarin ya faru ne a ranar jumaar yannkin rukunin gidaje na amazing grace da ke elepe a yankin ikorodu a jihar legas bayan wata zazzafar taƙaddama da ta ɓarke a tsakanin maauratan da ba su daɗe da aure ba

a yayin da rundunar yan sandan jihar legas take tabbatar da faruwar lamarin a wata sanarwa da mai magana da yawunta benjamin hundeyin ya fitar a ranar asabar ta bayyana cewa motunrayo ya daɓa wa matarsa mai shekara 25 wuƙa sau da dama yayin rikicin inda ya kulle ta a ɗaki sannan ya banka mata wuta

ya ƙara da cewa wanda ake zargin ya kuma raunata kansa bayan ya yi aikaaikar

ya ce jamian yan sandan da suka isa wurin su ne suka kashe gobarar da matashin ya kunna bayan da ya yi kisan inda suka gano gawar olajumoke da raunuka a jikinta

sanarwar ta ƙara da cewa an ankarar da rundunar ne ta hanyar kiran waya a ranar 4 ga oktoba a yankin ikorodu cewa wasu maaurata da suka yi aure ba da jimawa ba motunrayo olaniyi mai shekaru 30 da matarsa olajumoke mai shekara 25 an yi zargin sun kaure da faɗa a gidansu da ke yankin rukunin gidajen naamazing graceelepe ikorodu

inda mijin ya daɓa wa matar wuƙa kuma ya kulle ta a ɗaki sannan ya banka mata wuta inda ya raunata kansa

yan sanda daga sashin ikorodu sun amsa kiran da aka yi musu tare da kashe gobarar inda suka gano gawar olajumoke da raunuka a jikinta

kakakin yan sandan ya ci gaba da cewa an ceto olaniyi kuma aka garzaya da shi wani asibiti da ke kusa inda aka yi masa magani aka sallame shi kafin daga bisani yan sanda suka tsare shi

a cewarsa binciken farko da aka gudanar ya nuna cewa wanda ake zargin ya daɓa wa matarsa wuƙa ne a yayin rikicin tare da yi wa kansa ƙananan raunuka

an ajiye gawar matar a ɗakin ajiye gawa na babban asibitin ikorodu domin ci gaba da bincike in ji shi

a wannan bidiyon mun kawo muku waɗansu dabarun kasancewa cikin karkashi da ƙoshin lafiya yayin gudanar da ibadar kwanaki goman ƙarshe na watan ramadan mai a wannan bidiyon mun kawo muku waɗansu dabarun kasancewa cikin karkashi da ƙoshin lafiya yayin gudanar da ibadar kwanaki goman ƙarshe na watan ramadan mai albarka

ta ce mutuwarsa babban rashi ne a wajenta

hajiya hassana hasan a yanayi na kaduwa yayin tattaunawarta da aminiya ta bayyana yadda ta ji a ranta dangane da labarin rasuwar ɗanta na karshe

ta ce mutuwarsa babban rashi ne a wajenta domin shi ne wanda ke daukar dawainiyar rayuwarta

yan arewa musamma mace ballantana a ce a kano an san su da kamun kai da kaffakaffa

a yan makonnin nan bidiyon tsiraicin wasu jaruman tiktok mata yan arewacin sun yamutsa hazo

dambarwar bidiyon yan tiktok din daga jihar kano ya sa yawancin masu tsokaci kan wannan lamari nuna damuwa da diga aya kan dalilan yin irin wannan abin assha da kuma yaduwarsu

a makon jiya aka yi fama da dambar bidiyon tsiraicin hafsat baby wanda ya tayar da kura

dambarwar babiana bidiyon tsiraicin yar tiktok da ya fara fito tayar da kura a yan makonnin nan shi ne na babiana wadda aka fi sani da queen of update inda bidiyon ya fito bayan yan makonni da mutuwar aurenta

wannan ya sa ake ganin wuce gona da irin da yan tiktok mata daga arewa suke yi akwai alamar kidahumanci da sunan neman mabiya ko kuma daurin gindi da kuma uwauba rashin tunanin ranar gobe

a hirar da aka yi da ita kan dambarwar babiana ta yi ikirarin cewa wasu ne suka yi mata barazana domin ta ba su makudan kudade ko su saki bidiyon nata duniya ta gani ita kuma ta ce shege ka fasa shi ne suka yada bidiyon

tambayar da amsarta ta kasa samuwa ita ce wa ya dauki bidiyon mene ne dalili sannan ya aka yi ya shiga hannunsu

hafsat baby ta yamutsa hazo ana cikin wannan cakwakiya kuma a makon jiya kafofin sada zumunta suka sake daukar zafi bayan fitar da bidiyon wata yar tiktok a kano hafsat baby

a safiyar litinin da ake hutun ranar takutaha a jihar ce babban kwamandan hukumar hisbah sheikh aminu ibrahim daurawa ya wallafa bidiyon wasu mata da hukumar ta cika hannu da su ciki har da hafsat baby

amma daga bisani malamin ya cire bidiyon lamarin da ya haifar da cecekuce

aminiya ta nemi jin dalili inda babban daraktan hukumar abba said sufi ya shaida mata cewa hukumar ta gano cewa wadda aka kaman ba hafsa ba ce sai dai suna kama har a yanayin jikinsu

sai dai ya ce suna hakon hafsa domin ganin ta girbi abin da ta shuka

as online trading continues to grow in popularity many new platforms are emerging and quotex is one that has gained attention especially for those interested as online trading continues to grow in popularity many new platforms are emerging and quotex is one that has gained attention especially for those interested in binary options trading

however diving into the world of trading can be overwhelming and its essential to know what to consider before getting started

if youre thinking of using quotex here are some key things to keep in mind to help you navigate this trading platform effectively

quotex is a binary options trading platform that allows traders to speculate on the price movements of various assets including currencies commodities and stocks

the main allure of binary options is their simplicity you either predict that the price will rise or fall within a specified time frame

if you are correct you earn a profit if not you lose your investment in that trade

while this might seem straightforward successful trading requires a solid understanding of the market and sound strategies

before jumping into quotex its crucial to understand themechanics of binary options trading

unlike traditional trading where you own an asset binary options are purely speculative

this means you need to have a good grasp of market trends price movements and risk management strategies

spend some time learning about how binary options work and familiarize yourself with the different types of options available

creating an account on quotex is relatively easy

youll need to provide some basic information like your name and email address

however before you start trading make sure you verify your account

this often involves providing identification and proof of residence

verifying your account not only complies with regulations but also enhances your security on the platform

one of quotexs standout features is its demo account

this is a fantastic resource for beginners allowing you to practice trading without any financial risk

use this opportunity to familiarize yourself with the platforms features test your trading strategies and learn how to read charts and indicators

taking advantage of the demo account can build your confidence and prepare you for live trading

effective risk management is critical in trading especially in binary options where the potential for quick gains can be enticing

a common rule is to only risk 12 of your total money on one trade

this approach helps to protect your account from significant losses

additionally consider setting stoploss limits to automatically close trades that move against you further safeguarding your investment

understanding market analysis is vital for making informed trading decisions

there are two primary types of analysis you should become familiar with technical analysis and fundamental analysis

technical analysis is about looking at price charts and using tools to find trends and patterns

on the other hand fundamental analysis looks at economic indicators news events and other factors that can impact asset prices

a combination of both techniques can provide a more comprehensive view of the market

a welldefined trading strategy can make a significant difference in your success

start by determining your trading goalswhether youre looking for shortterm gains or a more extended trading approach

identify specific assets you want to trade and develop a plan for entering and exiting trades based on your analysis

having a clear strategy helps you remain focused and disciplined reducing impulsive decisions based on emotions

trading can evoke strong emotions ranging from excitement to anxiety

its essential to maintain emotional discipline and stick to your trading plan

avoid chasing losses or making hasty decisions based on fear or greed

if a trade doesnt go your way take a step back and analyze the situation rather than trying to recover losses immediately

emotional control is crucial for longterm success in trading

the financial markets are always changing influenced byeconomic news geopolitical events and market trends

staying informed about these factors can help you make more educated trading decisions

follow reputable financial news sources and consider joining online trading communities where you can share insights and learn from other traders

trading is a skill that requires ongoing education and adaptation

take advantage of the educational resources available on quotex including tutorials webinars and articles

as you gain more experience regularly review your trading performance and learn from your successes and mistakes

this continuous learning mindset can significantly enhance your trading skills over time

conclusion quotex presents an accessible platform for those interested in binary options trading

however entering the world of trading requires careful consideration and preparation

by understanding the mechanics of binary options utilizing the demo account managing your risks and developing a solid trading strategy you can set yourself up for success

remember trading is not just about making quick profits its a journey that involves learning discipline and emotional control

with the right approach you can navigate quotex confidently and make the most of your trading e xperience

happy trading

lets break down what you really need to know about binomo to help you make an informed decision

if youre thinking about getting into online trading youve probably heard of binomo

its one of those platforms that seems to pop up everywhere and for good reason

many people are drawn to it but before you jump in lets break down what you really need to know about binomo to help you make an informed decision

what exactly is binomo

binomo is an online platformthat allows users to engage in trading binary options

so what does that mean

essentially when you trade on binomo youre making predictions about whether the price of an asset like a stock currency or commodity will go up or down within a specific timeframe

if you guess right you earn money if you guess wrong you lose your investment for that trade

this straightforward approach can be appealing but it also means you need to know what youre doing to avoid unnecessary losses

why people love binomo understanding the risks now lets talk about the flip side

while binomo offers some great opportunities trading is risky

you can lose your entire investment on a single trade especially if youre not careful

its essential to do your homework stay informed about market trends and never invest more than you can afford to lose

this isnt just a hobby it can have real financial consequences

creating a game plan if you want to succeed on binomo having a solid trading strategy is crucial

many traders use technical analysis which involves looking at price charts and trends to make predictions

understanding concepts like support and resistance moving averages and candlestick patterns can really help you make smarter trades

start small and be patient if youre new to all this start with small investments

this approach allows you to learn without risking too much money upfront

as you get more comfortable and start to understand how the platform works you can gradually increase your investment

remember trading isnt a getrichquick scheme

it takes time patience and practice

connect with others dont forget that you have support during this journey

binomo has a community of traders where you can share experiences and seek advice

engaging with others can provide insights you might not have considered and can make the learning process a lot more enjoyable

plus its always nice to know youre part of a community

wrapping it up so are youthinking about trading on binomo

it can be an exciting and potentially rewarding venture but make sure you approach it with the right mindset

understand the platform acknowledge the risks and dont hesitate to use the resources available to you

with the right preparation and a willingness to learn you can make the most of your trading experience on binomo

ready to take the leap

your trading journey is waiting

za a riƙa karɓar harajin kashi 5 cikin 100 kan kuɗaɗen shiga na caca da cinikin caca ko kasuwancinta

a kwanakin baya ne kwamitin shugaban ƙasa kan sake fasalin kasafin kuɗi da haraji ƙarƙashin jagorancin mista taiwo oyedele ya gabatar da ƙudirin doka ga majalisar zartarwa ta tarayya wanda daga bisani aka amince tare da miƙa ta ga majalisar dokoki ta ƙasa domin amincewa

kwamitin wanda ke da alhakin daidaita yawan haraji a dukkan matakai na gwamnati yana da alhakin haɗe ayyukan tattara kuɗaɗen shiga tare da sabunta tsarin haraji da sauƙaƙa tsarisa gami da amfani da fasaha don tara kuɗaɗen shiga

an ɗora wa kwamitin ne alhakin sauya hanyoyin samar da kuɗaɗen shiga don samun cigaba mai ɗorewa da nufin cim ma aƙalla kashi 18 cikin 100 na harajin a cikin shekaru uku masu zuwa wato nan da 2026

daga baya a farkon watan oktoba 2024 shugaba bola ahmed tinubu ya miƙa ƙudirin sabuwar dokar haraji ta ƙasa ta 2024 ga majalisar dokoki ta ƙasa

a wannan yanayi darajar abin da za a karɓi haraji a kansa ya haɗa da jimillar laakarin da aka y da kuma harajin ɓat na kasuwancin da ya shafi kuɗi ko kuma darajar kasuwancin da ba na kuɗi ba a kasuwa

hukumomin gwamnati na tarayya jiha da ƙananan hukumomi maaikatunsu hukumominsu da sauran wakilan da aka zaɓa ana buƙatar su karɓa ko riƙe harajin na ɓat su miƙa wa hukumar haraji kamar yadda aka tsara

sabon ministan ya ce zai tabbatar apc ta sake ƙwace jihar kano a zaɓen 2027

sabon ƙaramin ministan gidaje da ci gaban birane yusuf abdullahi ata ya ce an naɗa sa minista ne don ƙwato wa jamiyyar apc jihar kano a shekarar 2027

ata ya bayyana haka ne yayin ziyararsa ta farko zuwa kano bayan shiga majalisar zarstawa ta tarayya

yayin da yake magana da yan jarida ya ce naɗina ya fi shafar siyasa

apc ta rasa jihar kano kuma yanzu za ta karɓe jihar

babbar matsalar da za mu fuskanta tana kano ta tsakiya kuma ni daga nan na fito

ya ƙara da cewa ko da ni minista ne zan ci gaba da zama cikin wannan yanki

za mu yi aiki tuƙuru domin ganin apc ta karɓe ikon jihar kano kafin 2027

ata ya bayyana cewa burinsa ya fi shafar siyasa duk da cewa zai mayar da hankali kan aikinsa a maaikatar gidaje da ci gaban birane

zan yi aikina amma zan riƙa dawowa kano a kowane mako domin aikin da aka ba ni wajen cimma wannan buri in ji shi

ya gode wa shugaban ƙasa bola ahmed tinubu bisa naɗin da ya masa

ya ce muƙamin da aka masa ba shi kaɗai ya shafa ba har da alummar kano da ma najeriya baki ɗaya

wannan shi ne tabbacin da na bai wa shugaban ƙasa in ji ata

a shekarar 2027 kano za ta koma ƙarƙashin ikon jamiyyar apc

da zarar an kammala taron shugaba tinubu zai dawo abuja

shugaban ƙasa bola ahmed tinubu zai tafi saudiyya domin halartar taron haɗin kan ƙasashen larabawa da musulunci

za a fara taron ne a ranar litinin 11 ga watan nuwamba 2024 inda za a tattauna kan matsalolin da ake fuskanta a gabas ta tsakiya

hadimin shugaban ƙasa kan yaɗa labarai bayo onanuga ya sanar da hakan cikin wata sanarwa

ya ce shugaba tinubu zai yi magana kan rikicin israila da falasdinu inda zai jadadda buƙatar a tsagaita wuta da kuma nemo mafita

najeriya za ta kuma goyi bayan ci gaba da ƙoƙarin dawo da tsarin ƙasashen biyu a matsayin hanya mai ɗorewa ta samun zaman lafiya a yankin

onanuga ya ƙara da cewa wasu manyan jamiai za su raka shugaba tinubu ciki har da ministan harkokin waje ambasada yusuf tuggar da mai bai wa shugaban ƙasa shawara kan shaanin tsaro mallam nuhu ribadu

sauran sun haɗa da ministan yaɗa labarai mohammed idris da darakta janar na hukumar sirri ta ƙasa nia mohammed mohammed

bayan kammala taron shugaba tinubu zai dawo abuja

don haka hankali ya karkata a duniyar kirifto baki ɗaya lokacin da a ranar alhamis da ta gabata aka yi iƙirarin cewa wanda ya ƙirƙiro da bitcoin zai bayyana kansa a wani taron manema labarai

a watan oktoba wani fim da kamfanin hbo ya yi ya nuna cewa wani masanin bitcoin na kanada mai suna peter todd shi ne ya ƙirƙiro shi

matsalar da aka samu ita ce ya ce ba haka ba ne kuma duniyar kirifto ta yi watsi da wannan batun

mista todd ne na bayabayan nan a cikin dogon jerin sanayen wadanda ka iya zama satoshi kuma a ranar alhamis jerin sunayen ya ƙara tsayi

akwai shaawa mai yawa kan ko wane ne satoshi nakamoto saboda ya kasance wani ƙasurgumin mai sarrafa manhajoji wanda ya taimaka wajen kafuwar masanaantar kirifto a duniya

muryarsa da raayoyinsa za su yi matuƙar tasiri a kan masanaantar da ke da mabiya da dama a duniya

amma wani abu kuma shi ne a matsayinsa na mamallakin fiye da bicoin miliyan ɗaya na iya zama hamshaƙin mai kudi saboda yadda darajar kuɗin ta kai mataki mafi girma a halin yanzu

ganin wannan dimbin arzikin abin mamaki ne a ji cewar wanda ya shirya taron manema labaran na makon da ya gabata ya buƙaci sai na biya kuɗin kujerar halartar wannan muhimmin bikin

idan ina son zama a gaba sai na biya fan 100

zan kuma ƙara biyan fan 50 idan ba na son a ƙayyade adadin tambayoyin da zan yi

wanda ya shirya taron charles anderson har ma ya ƙarfafa min gwiwa da in biya 500 domin samun damar yin hira da satoshi a kan dandalin da za a gabatar da shi

na ƙi dai amincewa

mista anderson ya ce duk da haka ina iya halarta amma ya yi gargadin cewa ba lallai ne in samu wurin zama ba

amma daga baya mun gano cewa wurin zama ba ita ce matsalar ba

kimanin an jarida 12 ne kacal suka hallara a shaharren wurin da ake kira front line club wanda masu gudanar da wurin suka yi bayanin cewa sun bayar da ɗakin ne kawai ba wai suna tabbatar da sahihancin abin da zai gudana ba ne

cikin lokaci ƙalilan ya tabbata cewa mafi yawan waɗanda suka halarci taron suna waswasi kan lamarin

bayan gudanar da ƙaramin bincike lamarin ya bayyana cewa wanda ya shirya taron da kuma wanda ke kiran kansa satoshi suna fafatawa a wata sharia mai sarƙaƙiya kan zargin zamba mai alaƙa da iƙirarin zama satoshi

ba dai fara da ƙafar dama ba kuma abubuwa sun ƙara taɓarɓarewa daga nan

mista anderson ya gayyaci satoshi ya fito kan dandali

wani mutum mai suna stephen mollah wanda ya ke zaune shiru a gefe duk tsawon lokacin ya tashi ya furta cewa na zo nan don in faɗi cewa da gaske ni ne satoshi nakamoto kuma ni na ƙirƙiri bitcoin akan fasahar blockchain

a cikin saa guda da ta biyo bayan hakan an jarida sun kasance daga shiga halin nishaɗi zuwa na ɓacin rai saboda ya kasa ba da wata shaida kamar yadda ya yi alkawari domin gaskanta iƙirarin nasa

mista mollah ya yi alƙawarin cewa zai buɗe ya kuma yi muamala da bitcoin na farko da aka ƙirƙira wani abu da satoshi ne kaɗai zai iya yi

amma ya kasa yin hakan

na tafi tare da wasu an jarida cikin ɓacin rai babu abin da muka tafi da shi illa shakku cewa wannan ma zai kasance wani labarin ƙanzon kurege a yunƙurin da ake yi na tabbatar da ko wane ne satoshi

jerin sunayen waɗanɗa ba a yi nasaran tababatar da cewa su ne satoshi nakamoto ba yana ta ƙara tsayi gaske

a shekarar 2014 wani babban labari a mujallar newsweek ya ce dorian nakamoto ne wani baamurke ɗan asalin ƙasar japan da ke zaune a california ya ƙirƙiro da bitcoin

amma ya musanta hakan kuma daga baya an yi watsi da wannan iƙirarin

bayan shekara guda an jarida sun yi iƙirarin cewa craig wright wani masanin kwamfuta a australia shi ne satoshi

daga farko ya musanta hakan kafin daga baya kuma ya gaskata amma ya kasa samar da wata shaidar da za ta tabbatar da hakan

a lokacin bazara wata babbar kotu a birnin landan ta yanke hukuncin cewa labarin nasa na boge ne

asalin hotonreuters hamshakin attajirin fasaha kuma mai kishin harkar kirifto elon musk shi ma ya musanta cewa shi ne ya ƙirƙiro da bitcoin bayan wani tsohon maaikaci a ɗaya daga cikin kamfanoninsa spacex ya yi iƙirarin yiwuwar hakan

wannan ne ya kai mu ga tambayar cewa wani muhimmanci sannin wanda ya ƙirƙiro kuɗin ya ke da shi

darajar masanaantar kirifto a halin yanzu na nufin ya fi kamfanin google daraja

kuma ba za a iya tunanin cewa wannan kamfanin fasahar da zai taka muhimmiyar rawa a rayuwarmu ba tare da sanin wanda ya kafa ta ba kuma ya mallaki kaso mai tsoka a kamfanin ba

wataƙila akwai kyakkyawan dalili da ya sanya satoshi ya yi gum da bakinsa kan ko shi wanene

saboda bitcoin ɗin da ya mallaka yanzu ya kai darajar kimanin dala biliyan 69 kuma ba shakka za a sanyawa rayuwarsu da halayensa ido idan har an gano ko shi waye

peter todd ya bayyana kwanan nan cewa sanya masa ido da aka yi ya sa ya fara fargaba kan tsaron lafiyarsa

mutane da yawa a duniyar kirifto suna jin daɗin cewa harb yazu an kasa gano wannan sirrin

babu wanda ya san wanene satoshi kuma wannan abu ne mai kyau adam back ɗaya daga cikin masu sarrafa fasahar bitcoin da kuma wani da ake ganin zai iya zama satoshi ya wallafa a shafinsa na x cikin kwanakin nan

natalie brunel wata mai gabatar da shirin rediyo kan bitcoin ta na tunanin rashin sanin ko wanenne satoshi abu ne mai matuƙar muhimmanci

ta hanyar ɓoye ainihin ko waye shi satoshi ya tabbatar da cewa bitcoin ba zai sami shugaba ko wani da za a alaƙanta da shi ba wanda raayinsa zai iya tasiri a kan yadda ake gudanar da hadahada da kuɗin in ji ta

wannan yana bawa mutane damar amincewa da bitcoin a matsayin tsari maimakon alakanta shi da wani mutum ko kamfani

carol alexander farfesar hadahadar kuɗi a jamiar sussex wadda ke ba da laccoci kan tarihin bitcoin ba ta da tabbas

a raayinta hayaniyar da ake yi kan ko wanene satoshi nakamoto na ɗauke wa mutane hankali kan yadda za su binciki lamarin yiwuwar yadda kuɗaɗen kirifto za su yi babban tasiri kan yadda ake gudanar da alamuran tattalin arziki a duniya

yayin da na bar frontline club na rasa abin da zan iya tabbatarwa daga wannan taron manema labaran illa abu guda ɗaya

a yanzu dai kuma watakila har abada za dai a ci gaba da neman ko wanene satoshi

ka zalika ya nuna damuwa kan matsalar kayan agaji a rikicin na gabas ta tsakiya

a matsayinmu na wakilai daga ƙasashen da suke mutunta adalci da mutuncin ɗan adam da kuma kare rayukan mutane muna da aikin da ya rataya a kanmu na ganin an dauki matakn dakatar da rikicin cikin gaggawa

ba kawai raayin diflomasiyya ba ne da ya yi daidai da abin da na yi amanna da shi wannan raayi ne da yake cikin dokokin daidaito da kuma fahimtar juna

duk munsan cewa wannan rikicin ba wai ya fara ba ne a ranar 7 ga watan oktoba na 2023 ba

amma za a cimma wannan sulhu ne ta hanyar kowa ya sarayar da wani abu da yake jin mallakinsa ne

wannan rikici na da dogon tarihi da matuƙar muni wanda ya haifar da rubuwar kawuna cikin ƙanƙanin lokaci

an riƙa yaɗa hotunan wannan rikici da ya ƙi ci ya ƙi cinyewa masu ɗaga hankali a wayoyi a faɗin duniya

don haka akwai buƙatar samar da sabbin hanyoyin samar da zaman lafiya ba tare da bata lokaci ba in ji shi

ya yaba wa yariman saudiyya mai jiran gado kan shirya taron wanda ya bayyana a matsayin mai muhimmanci kuma zai ba da damar sabunta diflomasiyya da kuma samar da zaman lafiya mai ɗorewa

hanyar sasancin za ta iya zama cike da ƙalubale amma za a yi ta cikin tattaunawar gaskiya domin fahimtar juna

amma ƙasashen duniya na da damar kawo sabbin hanyoyin kawar da wannan ƙalubale

in ji shugaban najeriyan

harin da hamas ta kai wa israila ranar 7 ga watan oktoban 2023 ya janyo mutuwar mutum aƙalla 1200 da kuma yin garkuwa da kusan 251

tun bayan nan israila ta kaddamar da mamaya kan zirin na gaza inda ta kashe sama da mutum 43000 waɗanda yawancinsu mata ne da kuma ƙananan yara

6 1 laifin wa

shehu t abdullahi wasu samari su uku umar da salman da hudu

suna zaune a bakin titi suna zolayar masu wucewa ko su tsokani budurwar da ba su san ta ba

kusa da su wata aramar yarinya ce take o arin tsallake hanya tana ta kaikomo amma su samarin nan ba wanda ya yi yunƙurin tsallakar da ita

wata mota irar jeep ta tsaya kusa da su wani mutum mai kimanin shekaru hamsin ya fito daga motar ya je ya kama hannunta ya tsallakar da ita kafin ya tafi ya juya ya kalli matasan nan ya ce musu kuna kallon yarinya tana o arin tsallakawa ba za ku taimake ta ba

duk suka sunkuyar da kai saboda ba su da ta cewa

ya shiga motarsa ya yi tafiyarsa

waye wannan

umar ya tambaya

salman ya amsa masa ba ka san alhaji sani ba

ai shi ne ake sa ran zai tsaya takarar ɗan majilisar wakilai

hudu yace kawai mu je gun sa mu tatsi rabonmu

duka suka amsa gaskiya ya kamata mu je

shigarsu falon alhaji sani ke da wuya suka tarar da shi yana zaune tare da yayansa ya marabce su

bayan sun zauna ne sai umar ya soma yi masa magana

ranka ya da e mu ne ka yi wa nasiha da safe bayan ka tafi shi ne muka zo mu maka godiya kuma mu nuna maka goyon bayanmu game da takararka

alhaji sani ya kalle su ya ce na yi farin ciki da hakan amma meye sanaarku

duk suka sunkuyar da kai saboda ba mai sanaa a cikinsu

umar ne ya aga kai ya ce ranka ya daɗe ai shi ne dalilin zuwanmu saboda mu ro e ka ka ba mu jari mu soma sanaa

7 alhaji sani ya sake kallon su ya ce to na ji zan ba ku jari amma da shara i suka ɗago da kawunansu duka suka kalle shi fuskokinsu cike da annuri

ya ci gaba da cewa shara in shi ne za ku zo min da iyayenku

a wannar rana suka zo da iyayensu gidan alhaji sani

ni ne na ce su kira ku saboda sun zo min da bu atar jari kuma bai kamata yara kamar wa annan a ce an bar su ba sanaa ba

don haka zan saya musu babura su fara aca a

ar ashin kulawarku tunda ku ne iyayensu

in suka dage sai su samu jari su yi sanaar da suke so

alhaji sani ya saya musu babura ƙirar bajaj sababbi dukansu uku

a gida hudu ya ce wa iyayensa ni fa ba zan yi aca a ba

cikin ka uwa mahaifinsa ya ce to me za ka yi

hudu ya amsa sayar da ita zan yi in sayi aramar u d ku kuma in ba ku dubu goma kai da mama

mahaifin nasa ya tuna masa maganar alhaji sani amma dai ka ji abin da ya fa a muku ko

hudu ya kafe baba ni ba zan yi aca a ba mahaifiyarsa ta tsoma baki a karo na farko to ai sai ka rabu da shi tunda ya ce ba zai yi ba bai kamata a tilasta wa yaro yin abin da ba ya so ba

haka hudu da umar suka sayar da baburan nan suka sayo ananan robaroba u d suka soma watayawarsu a gari suna guje guje lungu da sa o suka zama abin shaawa cikin abokansu

salman ne ka ai ya bi maganar alhaji sani da ta iyayensa ya fara aca a da babur insa

mai tattasai wani ri a en mai safarar waya ne da ya yi aurin suna cikin harkar waya

saboda ku in da ke shigo masa da kuma yadda matasa suke bin sa don ba ya yashin kashe musu ku i ko wato su daga hannun yan sanda

ganin haka ya sa shi shaawar zama an takarar majalisar wakilai wadda ake so alhaji sani ya tsaya

kamar wasa matasa suka tare jikinsa saboda ku in da yake bulbularwa

8 lokacin da mai tattasai ya ji labarin saya wa su umar babura sai ya sa aka kira su ya ce zai taimake su amma za su ri a kasuwanci tare

suka amince suka zama masu kasuwancin waya da cune suka zama ri a un yan taadda masu yin barazana ga rayuwar duk wanda ba ya goyon bayan mai tattasai

lokaci guda suka yi suna a gari

amma banda salman don shi har ya soma aure dabbobi da kuɗin aca a

bayan siyasa ta ringintsime an tinkari za e sai alhaji sani ya soma fiskantar barazana daga gun hudu da umar wa anda suka zo har gidansa suka masa barazanar ransa suna ce masa kada ya ga ya ba su wasu babura wai su yi aca a sun yi kama da yin aca a ne kuma idan bai janye daga takarar ba to za su yanka mahaifinsa sun ba shi sati guda

alhaji sani ya kai arar su ga hukuma mai tattasai ya shiga ya fita ya fito da su

cikin dare suka haura gidan mahaifin alhaji sani da nufin aiwatar da abin da suka uduri aniya

amma ba su samu nasara ba saboda mutane sun sadaukar da kansu suna gadin gidan

shigowarsu ke da wuya aka kama su aka laka a musu an karen duka aka kakkarya su

wayewar gari umar ya ce ga garinku

hudu kuma yana samun sau i aka kai shi gidan jarun amma ya zama yana ingishi

mahaifin hudu ya zo gidan alhaji sani yaranku saboda ba za su fahimci muhimmancin abin da ya sa na saya musu baburan ba shi ya sa na ce su kira ku domin in sun ri e aikin za su amfani kansu su amfane ku

amma kuka yale su suka yi gaban kansu

ranka ya da e wallahi mahaifiyarsa ce duk abin da na ce yaron nan ya yi sai ta hana

alhaji sani ya ce wannan ba hujja ba ce

domin ita ma a ar ashinka take kuma kai za a tambaya game da su ran gobe iyama

salman ai ya shiga jamia kuma na masa al awarin duk lokacin da ya kammala zan sama masa aiki saboda tsayuwar iyayensa da bin umurnin iyayensa

aka yi za e alhaji sani ya lashe za e

9 2 gobe ta allah ce adamu ahmed yarma malam saddam da magoya bayansa na zaune a wani falo inda suke tattaunawa akan yadda za su ar are shiri don fuskantar za en gobe

magoya bayan malam saddam yawancinsu matasa ne da yawa daga cikinsu ma alibansa ne ya koyar da su a sakandare

kyakkawar tarbiyar da yake ba wa aliban nasa a kan kishin asa da yadda yake bayar da tarihin asar da gwagwarmayar da aka sha kafin kafuwarta da kuma bayan kafuwarta ya sanya wa alibansa son asa da kishin ta

tsoffin alibansa da suka zama wani abu a rayuwa da suke ganin irin malam saddam ake bu ata a siyasar yau sai suka yi karokaro suka saya masa tiketin tsayawa takaran shugaban aramar hukuma

duk da cewa malam saddam bai so ba amma kyakkawar manufarsa da ilimin da yake da shi a fannin gwamnati ta sa ya kar i tayin nasu

a daren yau da matasan suke ta shiryeshirye na ganin sun kasa sun tsare kuma sun raka uriunsu ba tare da an musu magu i ba suna tsakiyar tattaunawa sai kawai suka ji dirowar wasu samari cikin falon kowannensu ya aure fuskarsa da ba in yalle hannayensu ri e da adduna ba su jira watawata ba sai kawai suka hau saran su malam saddam da jamaarsa

nan take su ma suka mi e don kare kansu

da yan taaddar suka ga an kusa a ci arfinsu sai suka arce bayan sun yi nasarar jikkata da yawa daga cikin mutanen malam saddam

10 bayan komai ya lafa ne malam saddam ya ebe wa anda suka ji rauni ya kai su asibiti

duk da ba su san wa anda suka kawo musu hari ba malam saddam ya san cewa ba mai aikata haka in ba anladi ba

anladi shi ne shugaban aramar hukuma mai ci kasancewar ba abin da ya tsinana wa jamaa ya sa jamaa ba sa son sa

ba irin tarkon da bai ana wa malam saddam ba don ganin ya ga bayansa kafin a kai ga ranar za e

ba irin barazanar da bai yi masa ba a kan ya janye udurinsa na karawa takara da shi har ta kai ga anladi ya san yadda ya yi aka tsayar da albashin malam saddam wanda hakan ya jefa shi cikin mawuyacin hali ga iyali ga mahaifansa da suke ar ashinsa da sauran mutanen da suka dogara da shi

kai sai da ta kai ga ya sa an rusa gidan malam saddam wai an gina ba bisa aida ba amma hakan bai ta a damun malam saddam ba

a asibiti malam saddam ya kwana tare da majiyata magoya bayansa har gari ya waye

a can cikin gari kuwa ana can ana ta gudanar da za e

malam saddam ya ma manta da ana za e hankalinsa na kan magoya bayansa da suke fama da raunuka

da jamaa suka ji labarin harin da aka kai wa malam saddam sai hakan ya ara masa farin jini wa anda ba su da raayinsa ma suka za e shi lamarin dai ya zama kamar gobarar titi a jos

a wannan yanayi aka kammala za e matasa suka kasa suka tsare suka kuma raka uriunsu ba tare da sun bari an musu magu i ba

a yammacin aka sanar da malam saddam a matsayin wanda ya yi nasara garin gaba aya ya au murna da shewa mace da namiji babba da yaro kowa sai murna yake yi

bayan an rantsar da malam saddam ne matasa alibansa da sauran magoya bayansa ya zama ba su da burin da ya wuce ya au musu fansa irin cin kashin da anladi ya yi musu

shi ko anladi yana can cikinsa ya uri ruwa dama kawai yake jira ya samu ya gudu ya bar garin domin ya san ba yadda za a yi a ce malam saddam bai au fansar abin da ya masa ba

11 matasa da aliban malam saddam na nan suna jiran su ji an kama anladi ciyaman suka ji shiru har ta kai ga sun tuntu e shi a kan ya au musu fansa

da malam saddam ya ga haka sai ya tara su yake musu bayani yan uwana ya kamata mu sani ba na hau kujerar nan ba ne don aukar fansa ko ramakon gayya ba

kun mara mini baya ne don mu kawo sauyi akan irin mulkin zaluncin da aka jima ana mana

yanzu da muka sami dama kamata ya yi mu himmatu wajen kawo sauyi ba aukar fansa ba

shawarwarinku nake bu ata a kan yadda za mu tafiyar da gwamnatin nan yadda talaka zai amfana ba ruruta wutar aukar fansa ba wanda hakan ba abin da zai haifar mana in ba tashintashina da fa acefa ace ba

oƙari ya kamata mu yi mu ga mun kawo arshen tashin tashina a yankinmu wanda hakan shi zai ba mu kwanciyar hankali da damar samar da abubuwan more rayuwa domin ciyar da yankinmu gaba

da fatan za ku yi mini kyakkyawar fahimta

dukkansu jikinsu ya yi sanyi daga ranar suka saduda

malam saddam ya gayyato anladi tsohon shugaban aramar hukuma domin tabbatar masa da cewa babu wani sauran gaba

da farko anladi ya auka kama shi za a yi bayan ya zo ne cikin ar ar ya fahimci manufar taron daga nan jikinsa ya yi sanyi ya yi nadamar abubuwan da ya aikata a baya ya yi farin ciki matuƙa da irin tarbar da malam saddam ya masa na karamci da nuna yafiya

daga ranar suka ha a kai don kawo wa yankin abubuwan ci gaba fa acefa ace ya are

anladi tsohon ciyaman ya jinjina wa malam saddam ganin yadda ya manta da duk irin etar da ya shirya masa a baya maimakon yanzu da ya sami damar ramako sai ya yafe masa

tabbas bahaushe ya yi gaskiya da ya ce gobe ta allah ce

12 3 matasa mu farka ayuba muhammad kumo hamis da ke zaune a kan turmi ya ce wa anwarsa ki auka kamar kin samu scholarship in nan ai kin gama komai tunda kika ci jarrabawar gaba aya

zan kar i takardunki in kai wa mai gidana honarabul an alalla a an majalisarmu kawai ki fara shiryeshiryen tafiya indiya

cikin karayar zuciya munira ta ce yaya na ji an ce fa sai an wane da wane ake bai wa anya zan hamis ya katse ta ni za a nuna wa uwa a gindin murhu kin manta gwamnatin gaba aya na mu ne ni da nake da honarabul babu irin wahalar da ban sha masa ba ke kin sani ni ne jagora a harkar daba a garin nan don haka ba indiya ba ko ingila ce honarabul zai samar miki albarkacina

honarabul an alalla a na zaune cikin ayataccen falonsa shi da mataimakinsa suna tattaunawa hamisu ya shigo falon sanye da hula hana sallah ya sami wuri a asa ya zauna ya cire hular ya ajiye a gefensa sannan ya kwashi gaisuwa

honarabul ya amsa cikin shewa ya ce

ka ga an halak auna hadarin daji yanzu haka maganarka muke

hamisu ya yi murmushin jin da i ya da a kwantar da kai

allah dai ya biya honarabul mai tazarce

kana gida muna maka ya i wallahi

duk wanda ya shiga hanyarka sai mun aika shi inda ya dace

honarabul ya yal yale da dariya ya ce shi ya sa nake jin da in aikinka auna

abin da nake so da kai shi ne so nake kafin ranar za e duk wata rumfa da ba tamu ba a baje ta ƙasa kar ta 13 kwana a garin nan kuma duk wadda ya yi yun urin tare ku ku yi maganinsa ko shi waye ne

don haka ne ka ai zai nuna wa abokan adawa cewa mun fi arfinsu su tsorata su gagara fitowa ranar za e

hamis ya amsa an gama honarabul

sannan ya mi a wa honarabul takardun anwarsa ya ce daman na ji ana raba scholarship zuwa asar indiya shi ne na kawo takardun anwata ita ma ta ci arziki

honarabul ya an ata rai amma ya kanne ya dube takardun samasama ya ga yadda munira ta cinye jarrabawar duka ya girgiza kai ya ce auna ai ka fi arfin an wannan alfarmar ka auka kawai ta samu

kai dai ka zauna cikin shirinka kai da mutanenka

da zarar lokaci ya yi zan nema ka

hamis ya yi godiya ya tashi ya fita

yana fita honarabul ya yi jifa da takardun cikin huci ya ce wa mataimakinsa ka duba samun wuri irin na talaka an iskan gari irin auna wai har ya yi wayewar da zai zo neman gurbin karatu wa anwarsa

sau uku yata fauziya tana rubuta jarrabawar nan tana fa uwa

mataimakinsa ya ce samun wuri ne kawai tunda yana da amfani a wurinmu ba za mu nuna masa ba za su samu ba yaudarar sa kawai za mu yi ta yi mu nuna muna matu ar o ari a kai

ashe duk abin da suke yi hamis yana laɓe yana sauraro ya dawo aukar hularsa da ya manta ransa ya yi matuƙar ɓaci ya fasa aukar hular ya fice daga gidan cikin huci

yana tafiya yana tunani cikin unar rai ashe duk bautar da yake yi wa mutumin nan kallon an iska yake masa ba yi da bambanci da karen farauta a wurinsa

tabbas anwarsa ta fi shi gaskiya domin ta sha fa a masa cewa bangar siyasar da yake yi ba abu ne mai kyau ba yau kam ya yarda

bayan ya dawo gida ne jikinsa a sanyaye ya fa a wa munira duk abin da ya faru

ta yi murmushi ta ce daman na san a rina kuma daman ni ban sa rai a kan zan samu scholarship ba

na ba ka takarduna ne don kawai mu ga gudun ruwan honarabul yanzu kam 14 ka yarda ai

tun daga ranar hamis ya ci alwashin ganin bayan tafiyar honarabul an alalla a

ana dab da za e ne honarabul ya tara matasa a farfajiyar gidansa dukkansu ri e da makamai

honarabul ya yi musu jawabi akan abin da yake so su aikata duk wanda ya yi o arin hana ku magu i ku kawar da shi ku aika mutum inda ba a dawowa

ni kuma zan ci gaba da ba ku duk wani abu da kuke so ku i da kayan aiki duka ku sha kuyi marisa ku more iya son ranku

matasan suka hau sowa cikin farin ciki a dai lokacin ne hamis ya matso gaba ya kalli honarabul ya ce yalla ai domin aiki ya yi kyau zai fi idan ka ha a mu da anka jabir domin ya taya mu kawar da abokan gaba sannan shi ma ya sha kayan maye ya yi marisa ya more

hamis bai gama rufe baki ba honarabul ya daka masa tsawa yana huci ya ce ashe ba ka da hankali an gaya maka ana zauna gari banza ne irinka

wanda ba shi da bambanci da karen farauta ka sani jabir ina ya fi arfin shiga wannan kacaniyar yana can london yana karatu

nan take honarabul ya sa mu arrabansa suka hau dukan hamis da yar yanuwansa suka kar e shi

matasan da ke wurin suka fahimci matsayinsu a dalilin su uldabakan da honarabul ya yi

ashe su ne ba su da gata yayansa kam sun fi arfin bangar siyasa

daga ranar hamis da sauran matasan suka watsar da bangar siyasa suka kama sanaa

ya zamana sai sun yarda da nagartan mutum kuma sai in sun ga yayansa a wurin kamfe suke yarda su goya masa baya

a haka kan matasa da yawa ya waye suka daina bangar siyasa suka farka ta hanyar kama sanaa

15 4 abin da ka shuka zainab husaini aminu da musa sun yi matu ar farin ciki da suka ji maigidansu alhaji jatau zai fito neman takara yanzu kam kakarsu za ta yanke sa a tun daga ranar da alhaji jatau ya kira su ya shaida musu udurinsa suka ora buri lokacin yin ku insu ya yi

alhaji jatau ya yi musu al awarin in ya ci za e zai saya wa kowannensu mota mai tsada

daga jin haka sai suka daina zuwa makaranta suka shiga bangar siyasa gadangadan har suka shiga sahun yan taadda ba wanda zai gaya musu su ji

tuni alhaji jatau ya yi musu hu ubar yadda za su yi a lokacin za e

ya kuma garga i yayansa na cikinsa akan kar su sake su fita ranar za e don kar a je a raunata su

ya bai wa aminu da musa ku a en da ba su taka kara sun karya ba don su tabbatar sun kawo uriun yankinsu ta ko wani irin hali ne

ana tsakiyar za e kuwa aminu da musa suka sace akwatin za e take yan sanda suka kama su sai gidan maza

al ali ya yanke musu hukuncin shekaru biyu a gidan yari abin mamaki alhaji jatau ko ya leƙa su

allah ya bai wa alhaji jatau nasara ya ci kujerar da yake nema sai ya tattara iyalansa suka koma abuja da zama ko labarin su musa ba ya yi

bayan shekara biyu suka fito daga gidan yari kai tsaye suka nufi gidan maigidansu alhaji jatau suka sami gidan a 16 rufe

hankalinsu ya tashi ba inda za su shiga ga iyayensu sun musu iyaka da su tun lokacin da suka shiga bangar siyasa

daga nan suka yanke shawarar tafiya abuja wajen alhaji jatau in banda rashin tunani irin nasu mutumin da bai je ya yi belin su ba ta yaya za su ni i gari su tafi har abuja gidansa

a haka suka kama hanyar abuja suka sami gidan alhaji jatau cikin sau i suka yi wa maigadi bayanin daga inda suka fito shi ko ya je ya yi wa alhaji jatau bayani

suna tsaye sai ga alhaji jatau ya fito kamar bai taɓa ganin su ba ya ata rai ya ce musu maza maza ku bar harabar gidan nan ko in sa a kama ku a mayar da ku gidan yari inda kuka fito

haka alhaji jatau ya fatattake su

suka shige cikin tsaka mai wuya domin ko ku in da za su koma gida ba su da shi suka shiga da nasani a lokacin da ba zai amfane su ba

suka tuna nasiha da garga in da iyayensu suka ta yi musu akan kar su yi wasa da damarsu su arar da samartakansu wajen bangar siyasa domin lokaci kamar wal iya ce in ya wuce ba ya dawowa

suka yi ta gallafiri a titi har yunwa tasa aminu ya yanki jiki ya fa i musa ya rasa me yake masa daɗi a duniyar nan

yana tsaye ya rasa yadda zai yi sai kawai ya ga wani mutum ya tsayar da motarsa a gabansu

musa ya hau ro on mutumin don allah malam ka taimake mu ɗanuwana ne ba lafiya

mutumin yana fitowa a motar musa ya ura masa ido ya ga ashe an siyasar nan ne alhaji ahlan wanda alhaji jatau ya kayar a za e ba irin cin mutuncin da ba su yi wa alhaji ahlan ba a lokacin yaƙin neman zaɓe

kunya ta kama musa ya rasa me zai ce wa mutumin da suka ci wa mutunci yau ga su a cikin ibtilai suna neman taimakonsa

alhaji ahlan da yake mutumin kirki ne kuma bai auki siyasa da gaba ba ya taimake su ya kai aminu asibiti ya yi ta jigila har aminu ya samu sau i da aka sallame su ne sai yake tambayar su dalilin zuwansu abuja

suka kwashe labarinsu gaba 17 aya suka labarta masa

ya girgiza kai ya ce gaskiya kun yi wasa da damarku wa ya faɗa muku mu yan siyasa muna da tabbas

yawancinmu da zarar mun hau kujerar mulki mantawa muke da al awuran da muka auka balle mutanen da suka sha mana wahala

don haka ina ba ku shawara da ku koma gida ku nemi gafarar iyayenku sannan ku kama sanaa na muku al awarin zan taimake ku

wannan abu da ya faru a gare ku ya zama muku izina nan gaba kar ku bari wani ɗan siyasa ya yi amfani da ku don ku yi masa bangar siyasa ku yi ta tayar da zaunetsaye

aminu da musa suka koma gida suka kuma nemi gafarar iyayensu sannan suka kama sanaa da taimakon alhaji ahlan suka daina bangar siyasa

daga ranar har mamaki suke idan suka ga matasa riƙe da gariyo da adda suna tayar da jijiyar wuya akan wani an siyasa da sunan bangar siyasa

alhaji jatau na zaune a falonsa yana shan ra a labari ya iso masa an kama ansa a mashaya fa a ya ha a shi da wata karuwa har ta kai ga ya da a mata wuƙa a ahon zuci ta mutu

yanzu haka yana magarƙama sannan yarsa da yake matuƙar so ta bi wani yaro an damfara sun bar asar take alhaji jatau ya yanki jiki ya fa i

18 5 ƙarshen alewa rashidat muhammad rashoo samarin biyu uban gishiri da ya'u na zaune a cikin kurkuku suna hira cikin farin ciki sakamakon gobe za su kammala waadinsu

suna tattauna irin muggan abubuwan da suka jima da shiryawa a kan za su aikata da zarar sun shaƙi iskar yanci

matasan biyu sun yi ƙaurin suna a harkar daba shi ya sa ma sabon ɗan takaran nan komared kabir ya zo ya yi belin su don su taya shi yaƙin neman zaɓe

usu kan aljan dake gefe wanda tunda suka fara maganar bai ce komai ba yana kallon su cike da mamakin duk da shekaru da suka ɓata a gidan yari amma har yanzu ba su daddara ba

yake kuma mamakin yadda za su biye wa wani ɗan siyasa don su masa bangar siyasa

usu kan aljan ya jima a gidan yari don su uban gishiri ma sun zo sun tarad da shi

yau ne ya juya ya kalli usu ya ce masa oga wai kai yaushe za ka fita ne

don in ba ina tsoron yin ƙarya ba sai in ce kafi shekaru goma a gidan nan

kan aljan ya yi murmushi ya ce tunda gobe za ku fita yau kam ya kamata in ba ku labarina

cikin ɗoki suka dawo kusa da shi suka zauna

kan aljan ya yi gyaran murya ya fara bana shekaruna ashirin da huɗu a gidan nan

asalin sunana usman abubakar na taso cikin sakalci da shagwaɓa kasancewar ni kaɗai ne ɗa namiji a wurin mahaifina hakan ya sa ba ya taɓa ganin laifina

komai na 19 aikata sai yace wai ai ni yaro ne in na girma zan daina

na zama ba mai faɗa mini in ji

na daina zuwa makaranta duk inda ake rikici ina wurin na yi ƙaurin suna wanda hakan ya sa yan siyasa nema na domin yi musu bangar siyasa

ya zamana duk wani ɗan siyasan da nake tare da shi to babu wanda ya isa ya nuna shi da yatsa saboda tsoro na da ake yi

duk irin baƙin jinin da na yi a wurin jamaa a hakan ummi take mutuwar so na kullum a cikin yi mini nasiha take a kan in daina wannar mummunar sanaa ƙaunar ta da nake yi ne kaɗai ya sa nake ɗaga mata ƙafa

an sha a kama ni a kulle manyan yan siyasa suna fito da ni

a haka har wata rana masu gidana suka sa na kashe wani mutum ashe mutumin yana ɗaya daga cikin jigajigan siyasar ƙasar nan

lokaci ɗaya gari ya ɗauka

iyayen gidana suka umurce ni da in gaggauta barin garin in ƙura ta lafa sai na dawo

har na shirya kayana zan gudu sai ga ummi

na sanar da ita batun tafiyata don ita ce kaɗai ba na ɓoye wa komai

ran ummi ya ɓaci sosai ta fashe mini da kuka ta hau mini nasihu masu karya zuciya ta tabbatar mini da cewa idan har a wannan karon ban shiryu ba ba ta ga amfanin rayuwarta ba ta mini barazanar cewa za ta kashe kanta kawai ta huta da irin baƙin cikin da nake tusa mata ita da mahaifiyata

a karon farko a rayuwata na ji na tsani kaina zuciyata ta karaya na ji na gaji da wannar ƙazantacciyar harka na ɗaga kai na kalle ta ta ƙara ba ni tausayi tun muna yara take so na ba irin zuga ta da ba a yi ba a kaina amma ba ta taɓa cire ran watarana zan shiryu ba

na yi murmushi na ce mata ki sa a ranki cewa daga yau na bar harkar daba zan koma mutum kamar kowa mu yi aure mu rayu cikin farin ciki

nan take hawayen farin ciki suka rinƙa ƙwaranya daga idanunta

daga ranar na daina karɓar duk wani umarni daga iyayen gidana na watsar da harkar daba

da yake ni ɗaya ne nake iya 20 aikata duk wani abu da suka saka ni komai hatsarinsa sai suka hau binciken silar shiriyata daga ƙarshe suka gano ummi ce sila

aka sa mana ranar aure ni da ummi wata rana ina gida ana gyara mini ɓangaren da zan zauna ni da ummi sai kawai babban yarona ya shigo da gudu yake shaida mini cewa wasu mutane sun tare ummi a hanyar makaranta sun daɓa mata wuƙa a ciki

a ruɗe na fita da gudu muna isa wurin muka tarar an garzaya da ita asibiti

na same ta kwance cikin jini shameshame na ƙarisa da gudu na durƙusa a kusa da ita ina hawaye

ta kalle ni ta yi murmushi ta ce na gode wa allah da ya kawo mini kai kafin in cika na yi burin ace na aure ka tun muna yara nake kallon ka a matsayin mijina ashe ba zan ga wannar rana ba na rufe mata baki na juya na kalli iyayenmu na ce musu su ɗaura mana aure

nan take suka ɗaura mana aure na riƙe hannunta tana mini murmushin farin ciki har ta cika

na yi kuka a ranar kamar raina zai fita muna fitowa yarona ya faɗa mini ai iyayen gidana ne suka sa a kashe ta cikin ɓacin rai da baƙin ciki maras misaltuwa na je na daddatsa su

jamian tsaro suka zo bataliya guda suka kama ni

kotu ta yanke mini hukuncin ɗaurin rai da rai

wannan shi ne labarina

na tuba a yanzu ko kiyashi ba zan iya kashewa ba

don haka kar ku bari yan siyasa su mayar da ku karnukan farautarsu

ba ni da wani buri da ya wuce yafiyar ubangiji ko ya sake sada ni da ummita a ƙiyama

uban gishiri da yau da ke zaune suna sauraron sa suka yi zugum jikinsu ya yi sanyi

labarin ba ƙaramin shiga jikinsu ya yi ba

cikin karayar zuciya uban gishiri ya ce oga tabbas labarinka ya sanyaya mini gwiwa lallai bangar siyasa ba abin yi ba ne

don haka ina fita sanaa zan kama dama ni tsohon ɗan acaɓa ne

yau da ke zaune ko motsin kirki ba ya yi ya ce ni kam ma ina ganin fasa fita zan yi don gaba ɗaya jikina ya mutu in ko na fita ba ni ba tayar da zaunetsaye samsam

21 6 an ci moriyar ganga aishatu ibrahim yahaya haƙiƙa ita siyasa rigar yanci ce kuma hanya ce da za a iya bi don kyautata rayuwar al'umma ta hanyar gina matasa domin su ne ashin bayan alumma kuma su ne manyan gobe

janwuya wani ta adarin matashi ne maras jin maganar iyayensa da ma duk wani wanda zai zaunar da shi ya fa a masa gaskiya

hakan ya sa ya yi aurin suna wajen fa acefa ace musamman akan bangar siyasa

janwuya ya auki siyasa da zafi wanda ta kai ga yana gaba da duk wani wanda ba jam'iyarsu aya ba

wannan ta adarancin da yake yi ne ya sa shi samun kusanci a wajen ubangidansa a siyasa wato alhaji badau

alhaji badau irin yan siyasan nan ne da su rasa kujerarsu gara a tayar da garin

yanzu haka shi ne an majalisa a yankin nasu kuma yana sa ran sake komawa a karo na biyu a wannan za en da ke aratowa

shi ya sa ya da a jawo janwuya a jiki

shi ko jan wuya da ya kashe zuciyarsa kullum yana nani e a gindin bishiyar gidan alhaji badau duk da cewa ba wani abin a zo a gani yake samu ba

jira kawai yake alhaji badau ya sa ya je ya ci mutuncin wani ko ya raunata wani

a haka har aka yi za e alhaji badau ya yi nasara a karo na biyu tare da gudunmawar jan wuya wanda shi ya yi ruwa ya yi tsaki wajen shirya magu i har ubagidansa alhaji badau ya kai ga nasara

22 bayan shu ewar lokaci ne ganin alhaji badau ya fara yi wa jan wuya wahala duk lokacin da ya je ofis wajensa sai a ce ayyuka sun masa yawa ya dawo wani sati idan ko gida ya je sai a ce alhaji badau ya dawo a gajiye ya je ya dawo gobe

da yake zuciyar jan wuya ta riga ta mutu wala ancin ba ya damun sa haka ya ci gaba da bin inuwar gidan alhaji badau ko a jikinsa

watarana musu ya ha a jan wuya da wani an adawa anadawar yake zayyano gazawar alhaji badau da yadda alhaji badau ya i taimakon jan wuya

gaskiyar da aka fa a wa jan wuya ta hasala shi ya kai wa an adawar naushi nan take fa a ya kaure a tsakaninsu

da yake jan wuya ba kanwar lasa ba ne kan ka ce me ya kir a wa anadawar naushi a ciki a take ya fa i bai sake ko shurawa ba

jamian tsaro suka kama jan wuya

bayan an auki lokaci ana buga shari'a aka yanke wa jan wuya hukuncin aurin rai da rai a gidan gyara hali

abin takaici tunda aka fara shariar har aka yanke wa jan wuya hukunci alhaji badau bai ta a zuwa inda yake ba

da na sani da uncin rayuwa suka bijiro wa janwuya a lokacin da nadamar ba za ta masa amfani ba

lokaci yana tafiya sauyi yakan zo wa al'umma musamman idan malaman addini suka ci gaba da shiga lungu da sa o don ya a daawa

bayan shu ewar wasu shekaru a gidan gyaran halin rayuwar jan wuya ta sauya ya yi nadama da kyakkyawar tuba ta silar babban limamin da ke karantar da su addini a gidan

har ta kai ga bayan shekaru da allah ya yi wa limamin rasuwa aka ga ba wanda ya dace da limanci da karantarwa a gidan in ba jan wuya ba wanda a yanzu aka mance da sunansa na jan wuya ya koma ainihin sunansa na yanka wato malam munzali

23 7 ba ar siyasa ahmad usman elnafaty abu ne sananne cewa siyasa tana da matu ar tasiri a cikin alumma na baya da na yanzu ta hanyar siyasar ce ake samun damar mulkar al'umma

sai dai kash a irin lokacin ne kuma wasu ke amfani da matasa suke ba su kayan maye da makamai domin tayar da tarzoma musamman don yin magu i a filin za e wanda hakan ke jawo wa matasan koma baya da lalacewa a rayuwarsu

alhaji haruna gwarzo da alhaji mudi bala su ne yan takarar kujerar gwamna a wannan karon

tsakaninsu babu jituwa kwatakwata kamar yadda kare ba ya jituwa da kura zafin adawarsu da zafin kansu ne silar jefa magoya bayansu cikin tsananin gaba da juna kullum a cikin yarfe da jifan juna da baƙaƙen maganganu suke wani lokacin ma har da fa acefa ace

hakan ya sa babban malamin addini a garin wato malam muslim yake ta fa itashi don ganin ya sulhunta tsakanin yan takarar

kullum a cikin nasiha da nusarwa yake

yana mai ba da shawarwari cikin hikima da tsantsar ilimi tare da bijiro da ayoyi da hadisan da suka yi tsokaci akan illar gaba da mummunan sakamakon da take haifarwa a cikin al'umma a addinance da duniyance

duk da irin wannan tsananin gaba da yan takarar ke yi bai hana yayansu shitu da talatu fa awa cikin kogin soyayya ba kasancewar suna karatu a jamia aya suna matu ar aunar juna kamar yadda iyayensu suke matu ar in juna

shitu da talatu sun sha u matu a sha uwar da suke ganin aya ba zai iya rayuwa ba in ba aya

a haka har lokacin za e ya zo kacaniyar kamfe ya ara tsamari magoya bayan yan takaran biyu suka yi ta kai wa junansu hari wa annan su rusa rumfar majalisar wa ancan su ma ayan su biyo aukar fansa abin dai babu da i ko ka an 24 a daidai wannan lokacin ne shitu da talatu suka sanar da iyayensu ala ar da ke tsakaninsu kowa yana ar ar a hakan dai suka sanar da iyayensu halin da suke ciki

duka iyayen biyu suka yi ba in ciki da jin haka suka kuma yi allahwadai da wannar ala a da ke tsakanin yayansu

suka tabbatar wa yayan nasu cewa in su ka ai suka rage a duniyan nan ba za su ta a yarda su aura musu juna ba

ba in ciki a wurin shitu da talatu ba zai misaltu ba suka shiga cikin tsananin damuwa har ta kai ga sun yanke wani mummunan hukunci wa kansu

kwatsam sai aka jiyo labarin cewa an ga shitu da talatu a bayan gari sun je sun rataye kansu allah ya taimaka wasu makiyaya suka hango su suka zo suka cece su

nan take iyayen nasu da jama'ar gari suka unguma zuwa bayan gari

cikin mutanen da suka je wurin har da malam muslim

nan take malam muslim ya yi amfani da wannar dama ya fara da yi wa shitu da talatu nasiha akan illar abin da suka yi o arin aikatawa ya nusar da su cewa da sun kashe kansu da makomarsu wuta ce

sannan malamin ya dawo kan alhaji haruna da alhaji mudi ya yi musu nasiha akan irin ba ar siyasar da ke tsakaninsu wacce ta kusa zama silar mutuwar yayansu

har ya buga musu misali da cewa yadda yaranku suke shirin kashe kansu haka yaran wasu suke kashe junansu a sanadiyar wannar ba ar gaba da kuke yi

nan take jikinsu ya yi sanyi suka saduda har ma suka rungume junansu suna masu nadamar abin da suka aikata a baya

ganin yadda jikinsu ya yi sanyi ne ya sa su ma magoya bayansu ajiye makamansu daga ranar aka sami zaman lafiya har aka bu e shiri a gidajen rediyo domin wayar da kan alumma kan illar gaba a cikin siyasa

ana dab da zaɓe ne alhaji garba habu ya shiga gidan rediyo neman alfarmar uri'un jamaa ya bayyana cewa shi ne yake tare da talakawa shi ya san damuwarsu ba wanda ba ya ma garin ba balle ya san halin da talakawa ke ciki

29 10 ina mafita

usman flash kowane yanki na alumma suna da nasu matsalolin da suke ci musu tuwo a warya a wasu wuraren hanya ce damuwarsu wasu kuma asibiti wasu kuma wutan lantarki

sun jima a cikin wannan yanayi na matsanancin ruwan sha

wakilansu na majalisa sun mayar da wannar matsala ta rashin ruwa a matsayin wani makami da kowannensu ya zo neman uria da shi yake kamfe

amma da zaran ya hau ba sa sake ganin sa sai lokacin za e ya sake zagayowa

nasir da musa sune matasan da suke da fa a a ji a harkar siyasa a garin kuma sun kasance a mabambantar jamiya wanda hakan ya sa kullum a cikin fa acefa ace suke

amma haka suke mantawa da tsohuwar abota da auratayya dake tsakaninsu suke tayar da zaunetsaye a yankin

ana nan wata rana abokinsu na yarinta usman wanda suke wa la abi da an boko ya dawo daga karatu

da usman ya gama nazartan halin da suke ciki sai ya yi amfani da iliminsa na siyasa da ya koyo a jamia ya fara wayar da kan mutane sannan ya je ya samu abokansa nasir da musa ya nusar da su yadda wakilansu suke amfani da su suna gwara kansu su kuma suna can suna kwasar ku i a majalisa

dukkansu suka gamsu da bayanansa suka nemi da ya fa a musu mafita

usman ya shaida musu mafita aya ce wasu matsalolin fa ba sai an jira gwamnati ta magance mana ba mu fara magance su da kanmu tukunna wanda idan kowa ya bayar da tallafinsa ka an ka an a ka ha a a matsayin aikin gayya za a iya tara ku in da za a tona rijiyar burtsatsai

an majalisan suna jin wannan labari ya zo cikin gaggawa ya hau aikin tona wasu rijiyoyin burtsasan aikin da ya kamata ya yi tun farkon hawansa bai yi ba sai yanzu da ya ga jamaa sun magance matsalarsu da kansu

suka yi fatali da an majalisansu suka za i usman an boko

tun daga ranar aka sami kyakkyawar wakilci a yankin

31 11 kujerar mulki ba tafi rai ba r a adam a daren jiya ne aka samu karon batta tsakanin magoya bayan jamiyar s r k da na jamiyar a u j a yayin da mutum hu u suka rasa rayukansu wannan labarin ya girgiza zu atan yan takarar gwaman guda biyu alhaji lami o farinwata da abokin hamayarsa malam shehu naallah

lamarin ya yi matu ar tayar da hankalin yan takaran kasancewar gaba ayansu ba masu son tashin hankali ba ne duk da cewa suna da bambancin raayi hakan bai sa sun auki siyasar da zafi ba suna da fahimtar juna musamman akan duk wani abu da zai kawo zaman lafiya a jahar

yau wa annan su kai wa wa ancan hari gobe aya angaren su je ramakon gayya

ba iya malam shehu da alhaji lami o ba ne labarin ya girgiza hatta babban kwamishinan yan sanda na jahar lamarin ya ta a shi

babban kwamishinan yan sanda ya fara musu bayani da cewa ha inmu 32 ne a matsayinmu na jamian tsaro mu samar da zaman lafiya da ingantaccen tsaro a jahar nan amma hakan ba zai yiwu ba sai da ha in kanku

na san ku mutane ne ba masu son tashin hankali ba domin ba ku da wani mummunan tarihi a wurinmu amma abin da ke aure mana kai shi ne yadda ake samun tashintashina a tsakanin magoya bayanku

don haka na tara ku a nan ne domin mu samar da mafita a kan fa acefa acen dake faruwa a cikin wannar jahar kafin za e

yan takaran biyu suka yi farin ciki da jin jawabin kwamishina

malam shehu na allah ya ce lamarin yana matu ar aga mini hankali idan na ji ana fitina a kanmu

ni da har na yanke shawarar zan ha ura da takarar gaba aya domin bai kamata a ce a kan karagar mulki ake kashe mutane ba abokina alhaji lami o shi ne ya danne ni a daren jiyan

alhaji lami o ya gya a kai ya ce tabbas haka ne ni a fahimtata ina gani wasu ne masu mummunan manufar suke mana ma ar ashiya

kwamishina ya girgiza kai alamar ya gamsu da jawabansu sannan ya ce tunda yanzu na da a fahimtar cewa ba ku da hannu a ciki ina son ku ha a gagarumin taro domin ku barrantar da kanku daga dukkan wani naui na tayar da zaunetsaye ku yi amfani da wannan damar wajen wayar da kan magoya bayanku ku nuna musu zamani ya sauya dabanci da sarasuka da kalare sun zama ƙauyanci

matasa su yasar da gariyo da adda su ri i biro da kafafen ya a zumunta don tallata gwanayensu da manufofinsu a ilimance

sannan kwamishinan ya rufe da cewa mu kuma daga yau za mu sa afar wando aya da duk wanda muka samu da tayar da zaune tsaye

haka kuwa aka yi malam shehu naallah da alhaji lami o suka shirya gagarumin taro a babban filin wasa na jahar suka sanya wa taron suna kujerar mulki ba tafi rai ba a taron ne suka wayar da kan magoya bayansu akan muhimmancin zaman lafiya da illolin tayar da zaunetsaye suka tabbatar wa jamaa gwara su rasa kujerar da ace an kashe mutum aya a sanadiyarsu

33 tun daga ranar mafi yawanci daga cikin magoya bayansu masu zafin kai suka yasar da makamansu suka fahimci cewa zamani ya sauya yanzu a arni na ashirin da aya ake don haka ya kamata danbarwar siyasar ma ta sauya
